<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kado.html>kado</a> (14737)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:cadeau.html>cadeau</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kado.html>kado</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kado.html>kado</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kadootje.html>kadootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***kaffer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaffer.html>kaffer</a> (26185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">كَافِر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kāfir</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">infidel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaffer.html>kaffer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaffers.html>kaffers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaffer.html>kaffertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">originally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A non-believer or an infidel from the Muslim viewpoint</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A black person, notably a (Southern African) Bantu.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stupid person, numskull</li></ol>

***kajuit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kajuit.html>kajuit</a> (26184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">kajüte</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kayhute</i>, of uncertain ultimate origin; possibly borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to Watkins, possibly a mix of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cabane</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">hutte</i>.  Other possibilities include <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cave</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hollow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kooi.html>kooi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a doublet of it.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kajüte</i>.  Also compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cahute</i>, which could be a borrowing.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kajuit.html>kajuit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kajuit.html>kajuiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kajuit.html>kajuitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cabin on a ship</li></ol>

***kakken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kakken.html>kakken</a> (16377)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cacken</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cacō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to defecate, soil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, either way presumably ultimately sound imitative.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kakken.html>kakken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to defecate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to (secrete) <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a> (notably solids)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trot slowly, lustlessly</li></ol>

***kalkoen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kalkoen.html>kalkoen</a> (4604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Calcoensche <a href = vnd.unilang:haan.html>haan</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Calcoen</i>, the then-used name for the Indian city <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Calicut</i>, modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Kozhikode</i>. Although the bird originated in the Americas, confusion arose due to its similarity to the <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">African guinea fowl</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> exported to and imported from India since the 15th century by Portuguese traders.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kalkoen.html>kalkoen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kalkoenen.html>kalkoenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kalkoen.html>kalkoentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>turkey, <i>Meleagris gallopavo</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">boskalkoen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pauwkalkoen</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kalkoen.html>kalkoen</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">כּלה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:kale.html>kale</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bride</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">כַּלָּה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kalá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bride</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. A relation with the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kallen</i> (“to chatter”, compare etymology 2 hereunder), <a href = vnd.unilang:claimed.html>claimed</a> in some popular-scientific resources, exists at most through secondary association. ***kalverliefde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kalverliefde.html>kalverliefde</a> (35973)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kalver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">calf, young bovine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefde.html>liefde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 17th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kalverliefde.html>kalverliefde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kalverliefde.html>kalverliefdes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">kalverliefden</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">puppy love</span>; a youthful, immature form of love often associated with young people.
<ul><li><b>1625</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cats.html>Cats</a>, "Wegh-wyser ten houwelijck uyt den dool-hof <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kalverliefde.html>kalverliefde</a></b>." ("Road sign towards marriage from the maze of <b>puppy love</b>"), in <i>Houwelijcx</i> (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://dbnl.nl/tekst/cats001jvan02_01/cats001jvan02_01_0205.php">DBNL</a>), in <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloten.html>Vloten</a> (ed.), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>Alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cats.html>Cats</a></i>, part 1, publ. by <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erven.html>erven</a> J.J. Tijl (1862), page 358.</li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kalverliefde.html>kalverliefde</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:psychologie.html>psychologie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a>, voorbijgaande <a href = vnd.unilang:verliefdheid.html>verliefdheid</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jeugdige.html>jeugdige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verliefdheid.html>verliefdheid</a>, jeugdliefde</li></ol>

***kam.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kam.html>kam</a> (7600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kamb</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kambaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Comb.png/250px-Comb.png" decoding="async" width="250" height="49" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Comb.png/375px-Comb.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Comb.png/500px-Comb.png 2x" data-file-width="1037" data-file-height="205" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:kam.html>Kam</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kam.html>kam</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kammen.html>kammen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kammetje.html>kammetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A comb, utensil to groom hair, fur etc.</li>
<li>(<i>anatomy etc.; by analogy</i>) A ridge, erect shape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cam</li>
<li>bridge (e.g. of a violin)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kameel.html>kameel</a> (12160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cameel</i>, older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kemel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">camēlus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάμηλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kámēlos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semitic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Semitic languages">Semitic</a></span> language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kameel.html>kameel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamelen.html>kamelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kameel.html>kameeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:politicus.html>politicus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echte.html>echte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kameleon.html>kameleon</a></b>: <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verandert.html>verandert</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeiteloos.html>moeiteloos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opinie.html>opinie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opnieuw.html>opnieuw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:partij.html>partij</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>That politician <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a true turncoat: he changes opinions effortlessly, now <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> switched parties again!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a> (371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cāmere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room, barn, house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kamara</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:camera.html>camera</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room, vault</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">καμάρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kamára</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vaulted chamber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamers.html>kamers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamertje.html>kamertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A room, a chamber.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with the user or owner specified</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> A bedroom.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaapkamer.html>slaapkamer</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> with the definite article, often not specified</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A living room.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huiskamer.html>huiskamer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">living</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woonkamer.html>woonkamer</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with the definite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A special, more luxurious living room (formerly) reserved for use on Sundays and holidays, found in old <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a> that <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> inhabited by relatively affluent people.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bestekamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pronkkamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">zondagskamer</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li>A chamber of a gun.</li>
<li>A chamber of parliament <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">legislative body</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A non-campus residence for students.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kot.html>kot</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">studentenkamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">studentenkot</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kam.html>kam</a></i>. Displaced earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kemmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kemben</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kemmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kemben</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kambijaną</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kambaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">comb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>to comb <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">use a comb to groom hair, fur etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">camp</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">campus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">open space; field</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>camp</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">camp</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">campus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">open space; battlefield</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kampen.html>kampen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kampje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>battle</li>
<li>tournament</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>In the Netherlands <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seldom used as a word to describe a battle, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevecht.html>gevecht</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more common. However, in Flanders this usage <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very common.
</p>

***kanaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kanaal.html>kanaal</a> (3686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">canael</i>, from older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">canel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">canal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">canālis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pipe, channel, canal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">canna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a>, cane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάννα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kánna</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akkadian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Akkadian language">Akkadian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="akk">𒄀</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="akk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qanû</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sumerian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Sumerian language">Sumerian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="sux">𒄀𒈾</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sux-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gi.<a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kanaal.html>kanaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kanalen.html>kanalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kanaaltje.html>kanaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>canal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">artificial waterway</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>gracht</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaart.html>vaart</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>television or internet channel</li>
<li>channel <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">narrow natural body of water</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:straat.html>straat</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>duct, pipe
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiding.html>leiding</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>duct-shaped tissue</li>
<li>frequency <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kanaal.html>Kanaal</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally not used for city canals, although such usage <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attestable. The usual term for those <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>gracht</a></i> in the Netherlands and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rui.html>rui</a></i> in Belgium.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kanjer.html>kanjer</a> (5520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">keniart</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">canjaert</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kangart</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kenjard</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cagnard</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A lazy and/or boastful person.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A quack, a <a href = vnd.unilang:charlatan.html>charlatan</a>.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">canker</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cancer</i>.
